21-23 Point Standard Decklists
==============================



 Posted in [PRO TOUR MAGIC ORIGINS](/en/events/coverage/ptori)
 on August 2, 2015 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/wizards_authorpic_larger.jpg)
By Wizards of the Coast










A total of 32 players earned between 21 and 23 points in the Standard rounds of Pro Tour Magic Origins. There were 25 players who earned 21 points (7-3) from Standard and seven who earned 22 points (7-2-1).




---

**The following players finished with 22 points (7-2-1) in Standard:**







#### Stephen Berrios


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-4098cd174d76e25cd40db66538ab4aba.txt?n=Stephen%20Berrios)
